<h1 id="层次化概念嵌入与追踪可解释图像分类的深度解读">层次化概念嵌入与追踪:可解释图像分类的深度解读</h1>
<h2 id="一、深入论文解读1000-1500字">一、深入论文解读(1000-1500字)</h2>
<p>这篇论文针对<strong>可解释图像分类</strong>中的一个关键挑战:现有方法在提取概念时忽略了概念间的<strong>层次结构关系</strong>,导致解释不一致。举例来说,当分类一张猫的图片时,理想的解释路径应该是"动物→哺乳动物→猫",但现有的稀疏编码方法可能会错误地提取出"交通工具"等与层次结构不符的概念(见图1)。</p>
<h3 id="核心创新hcep框架">核心创新:HCEP框架</h3>
<p>论文提出的**HCEP(Hierarchical Concept Embedding &amp; Pursuit)**框架包含两个核心组件:</p>
<p><strong>1. 层次化概念嵌入(§3)</strong></p>
<p>作者首先定义了理想的几何条件。给定一个概念层次树,论文提出两个关键约束:</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>良好聚类的同义词集(Well-clustered synsets)</strong>:通过命题3.1形式化了"子树包含性"和"兄弟锥体分离性"。具体而言,对于树中的每个节点<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>i</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">i</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.65952em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">i</span></span></span></span></span>,其所有后代节点的嵌入向量应包含在一个以<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msup><mi>a</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>i</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a^{(i)}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.888em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.888em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>为顶点、半角为<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>θ</mi><mrow><mtext>lev</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>i</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\theta_{\text{lev}(i)}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.04964em; vertical-align: -0.3552em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">θ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3448em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.5198em; margin-left: -0.02778em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">lev</span></span><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3552em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>的锥体内:<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><munder><mrow><mi>max</mi><mo>⁡</mo></mrow><mrow><mi>j</mi><mo>∈</mo><mtext>desc</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>i</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></munder><mi mathvariant="normal">∠</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msup><mi>a</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>i</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo separator="true">,</mo><msup><mi>a</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>j</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>≤</mo><msub><mi>θ</mi><mrow><mtext>lev</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>i</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\max_{j \in \text{desc}(i)} \angle(a^{(i)}, a^{(j)}) \leq \theta_{\text{lev}(i)}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.904em; vertical-align: -0.966em;"></span><span class="mop op-limits"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.43056em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.309em; margin-left: 0em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.05724em;">j</span><span class="mrel mtight">∈</span><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">desc</span></span><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class=""><span class="mop">max</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.966em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord">∠</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.938em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.938em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; vertical-align: -0.3552em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">θ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3448em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.5198em; margin-left: -0.02778em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">lev</span></span><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3552em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>同时,任意两个兄弟节点<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>j</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><msup><mi>j</mi><mo mathvariant="normal" lspace="0em" rspace="0em">′</mo></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">j, j'</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.946332em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05724em;">j</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05724em;">j</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.751892em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">′</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>的子树锥体不相交:<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">∠</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msup><mi>a</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>j</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo separator="true">,</mo><msup><mi>a</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msup><mi>j</mi><mo mathvariant="normal" lspace="0em" rspace="0em">′</mo></msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>&gt;</mo><msub><mi>θ</mi><mrow><mtext>lev</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>j</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msub><mo>+</mo><msub><mi>θ</mi><mrow><mtext>lev</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msup><mi>j</mi><mo mathvariant="normal" lspace="0em" rspace="0em">′</mo></msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\angle(a^{(j)}, a^{(j')}) &gt; \theta_{\text{lev}(j)} + \theta_{\text{lev}(j')}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.24248em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">∠</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.938em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.05724em;">j</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.827829em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.931em; margin-right: 0.0714286em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.5em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">′</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">&gt;</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.04964em; vertical-align: -0.3552em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">θ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3448em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.5198em; margin-left: -0.02778em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">lev</span></span><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.05724em;">j</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3552em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.04964em; vertical-align: -0.3552em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">θ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3448em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.5198em; margin-left: -0.02778em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">lev</span></span><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.05724em;">j</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.682829em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.786em; margin-right: 0.0714286em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.5em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">′</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3552em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>层次正交性与单纯形结构</strong>:受大语言模型几何研究启发,论文要求子节点与父节点的差向量正交于父节点本身,即<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msup><mi>a</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>j</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>−</mo><msup><mi>a</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>i</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">⊤</mi></msup><msup><mi>a</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>i</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>=</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(a^{(j)} - a^{(i)})^\top a^{(i)} = 0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.138em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.888em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.05724em;">j</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.138em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.888em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose"><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.849108em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">⊤</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.888em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span></span></span></span></span>。此外,同一父节点的所有子节点差向量应形成一个规则<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>b</mi><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(b-1)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">b</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span>-单纯形结构(其中<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>b</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">b</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">b</span></span></span></span></span>为分支因子)。</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p>论文在命题3.3中证明了<strong>深度-维度必要条件</strong>:要在<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msup><mi mathvariant="double-struck">R</mi><mi>d</mi></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathbb{R}^d</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.849108em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbb">R</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.849108em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">d</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>空间中嵌入深度为<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>L</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">L</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">L</span></span></span></span></span>、分支因子为<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>b</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">b</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">b</span></span></span></span></span>的层次结构,需要满足<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>d</mi><mo>≥</mo><mi>L</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>b</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">d \geq L + b</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83041em; vertical-align: -0.13597em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">d</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≥</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.76666em; vertical-align: -0.08333em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">L</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">b</span></span></span></span></span>。这是因为每增加一层,层次正交性约束会减少一个自由度,而嵌入<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>b</mi><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(b-1)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">b</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span>-单纯形需要<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>b</mi><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(b-1)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">b</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span>个维度。幸运的是,CLIP的768维嵌入空间远超WordNet的<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>L</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>12</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">L=12</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">L</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">12</span></span></span></span></span>和<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>b</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>25</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">b=25</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">b</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">25</span></span></span></span></span>,完全满足此条件。</p>
<p><strong>2. 层次化概念追踪(§4)</strong></p>
<p>在概念恢复阶段,作者提出了<strong>层次化字典构造</strong>方法。字典<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>D</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">D</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">D</span></span></span></span></span>定义为:<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mi>D</mi><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">[</mo><msup><mi>a</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo separator="true">,</mo><mo>…</mo><mo separator="true">,</mo><msup><mi>a</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>b</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo separator="true">,</mo><msup><mi>a</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>j</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>−</mo><msup><mi>a</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mtext>par</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>j</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo separator="true">,</mo><mo>…</mo><mo separator="true">,</mo><msup><mi>a</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>j</mi><mi>k</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>−</mo><msup><mi>a</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mtext>par</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>j</mi><mi>k</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo stretchy="false">]</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">D = [a^{(1)}, \ldots, a^{(b)}, a^{(j_1)} - a^{(\text{par}(j_1))}, \ldots, a^{(j_k)} - a^{(\text{par}(j_k))}]</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">D</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.188em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.938em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mtight">1</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="minner">…</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.938em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">b</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.938em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.05724em;">j</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.317314em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.357em; margin-left: -0.05724em; margin-right: 0.0714286em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.5em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.143em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.13244em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.938em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">par</span></span><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.05724em;">j</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.317314em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.357em; margin-left: -0.05724em; margin-right: 0.0714286em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.5em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.143em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose mtight">))</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="minner">…</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.938em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.05724em;">j</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3448em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.34877em; margin-left: -0.05724em; margin-right: 0.0714286em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.5em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.03148em;">k</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151229em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.188em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.938em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">par</span></span><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.05724em;">j</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3448em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.34877em; margin-left: -0.05724em; margin-right: 0.0714286em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.5em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.03148em;">k</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151229em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose mtight">))</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>前<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>b</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">b</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">b</span></span></span></span></span>列是根节点的子节点嵌入,后续列是所有非根节点与其父节点的差向量。这种设计的巧妙之处在于:<strong>差向量本身就具有可解释的语义意义</strong>,例如"白色"这一概念对应于"北极熊-熊"的差向量。</p>
<p>基于此字典,论文提出**层次化正交匹配追踪(Hierarchical OMP)<strong>算法(算法1)。该算法有两个关键改进:(1)在每次迭代中,仅从当前最深节点的子节点中扩展稀疏支持集;(2)使用</strong>束搜索(beam search)<strong>维护多个假设,避免早期错误决策传播。命题4.1证明,在假设每次选择的原子都在正确支持集中时,Hierarchical OMP的</strong>精确恢复系数(ERC)**成功区域严格大于标准OMP,这为算法的优越性提供了理论保证。</p>
<h3 id="实验验证">实验验证</h3>
<p>论文在合成数据和三个真实数据集(ImageNette、ImageNet、CIFAR-100)上进行了全面实验:</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>合成实验</strong>(图5):在分支因子<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>b</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>3</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">b=3</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">b</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">3</span></span></span></span></span>、深度<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>L</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>7</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">L=7</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">L</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">7</span></span></span></span></span>、维度<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>d</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>50</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">d=50</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">d</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">50</span></span></span></span></span>的设置下,Hierarchical OMP在支持集精度和召回率上始终优于标准OMP,证明了层次结构的有效性。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>ImageNet实验</strong>(表1):在低样本设置(12-shot)下,HCEP的分类准确率达到<strong>52.1%</strong>,支持集精度为<strong>71.2%</strong>,召回率为<strong>71.8%</strong>,全面超越OMP(45.8%/15.6%/36.6%)和层次化NN(28.1%/47.9%/44.1%)等基线。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>跨模型泛化</strong>(图11):将CLIP替换为SigLIP后,HCEP仍展现出类似的改进,证明了框架的普适性。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>几何验证</strong>(图6-7):实验证实CLIP嵌入确实满足层次正交性(子-父差向量与父节点的余弦相似度接近0)和良好聚类性质(大多数分支紧密聚类且分离良好)。</p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<h2 id="二、研究目标与实际意义">二、研究目标与实际意义</h2>
<h3 id="研究目标">研究目标</h3>
<ul>
<li><strong>核心问题</strong>:现有可解释模型在提取概念时忽略层次结构,导致解释不一致(如将"猫"解释为包含"交通工具")</li>
<li><strong>解决方案</strong>:将概念层次结构嵌入稀疏编码框架,确保提取的概念形成一致的根到叶路径</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="产业意义">产业意义</h3>
<ul>
<li>在医疗诊断、自动驾驶等高风险领域,可解释性对建立信任至关重要</li>
<li>低样本学习场景下,HCEP的优势尤为明显(12-shot下优于所有基线)</li>
<li>可扩展至现有的高质量层次结构(如RadLex、iNaturalist)</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<h2 id="三、模型方法详解">三、模型方法详解</h2>
<h3 id="层次化概念嵌入模型">3.1 层次化概念嵌入模型</h3>
<p><strong>命题3.1(良好聚类保证唯一父节点分配)</strong></p>
<p>假设对层次结构中所有节点满足以下几何条件:</p>
<ol>
<li>
<p><strong>子树包含性</strong>:<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><munder><mrow><mi>max</mi><mo>⁡</mo></mrow><mrow><mi>j</mi><mo>∈</mo><mtext>desc</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>i</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></munder><mi mathvariant="normal">∠</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msup><mi>a</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>i</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo separator="true">,</mo><msup><mi>a</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>j</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>≤</mo><msub><mi>θ</mi><mrow><mtext>lev</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>i</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mi>i</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><mo>…</mo><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>N</mi><mi>L</mi></msub><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>2</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\max_{j \in \text{desc}(i)} \angle(a^{(i)}, a^{(j)}) \leq \theta_{\text{lev}(i)}, \quad i = 1, \ldots, N_L \quad (2)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.904em; vertical-align: -0.966em;"></span><span class="mop op-limits"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.43056em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.309em; margin-left: 0em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.05724em;">j</span><span class="mrel mtight">∈</span><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">desc</span></span><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class=""><span class="mop">max</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.966em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord">∠</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.938em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.05724em;">j</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≤</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.04964em; vertical-align: -0.3552em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">θ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3448em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.5198em; </li>
<li>
<p><strong>兄弟锥体分离性</strong>:对任意父节点<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>i</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">i</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.65952em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">′</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">∈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">chi</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">i</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span>:<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">∠</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msup><mi>a</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>j</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo separator="true">,</mo><msup><mi>a</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msup><mi>j</mi><mo mathvariant="normal" lspace="0em" rspace="0em">′</mo></msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>&gt;</mo><msub><mi>θ</mi><mrow><mtext>lev</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>j</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msub><mo>+</mo><msub><mi>θ</mi><mrow><mtext>lev</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msup><mi>j</mi><mo mathvariant="normal" lspace="0em" rspace="0em">′</mo></msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msub><mo>=</mo><mn>2</mn><msub><mi>θ</mi><mrow><mtext>lev</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>i</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msub><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>3</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\angle(a^{(j)}, a^{(j')}) &gt; \theta_{\text{lev}(j)} + \theta_{\text{lev}(j')} = 2\theta_{\text{lev}(i)-1} \quad (3)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.24248em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">∠</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.938em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; vertical-align: -0.3552em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">θ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3448em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.5198em; vertical-align: -0.3552em;"></span><span class="mord">2</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">θ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3448em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.5198em; </li>
</ol>
<p>则兄弟节点的子树不相交,每个节点有唯一父节点。</p>
<p><strong>命题3.2(几何半角递减调度)</strong></p>
<p>若半角满足:<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>θ</mi><mrow><mi>l</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msub><mo>≤</mo><mi>min</mi><mo>⁡</mo><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi>r</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mn>1</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><mi>b</mi><mo stretchy="false">}</mo><msub><mi>θ</mi><mi>l</mi></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mi>r</mi><mo>∈</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>0</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><mn>1</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><mn>2</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>4</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\theta_{l+1} \leq \min\{r, 1/b\}\theta_l, \quad r \in (0, 1/2) \quad (4)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.902771em; vertical-align: -0.208331em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">θ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.02778em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.01968em;">l</span><span class="mbin mtight">+</span><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.208331em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≤</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mop">min</span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">r</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord">1/</span><span class="mord mathnormal">b</span><span class="mclose">}</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">θ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.02778em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.01968em;">l</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 1em;"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">r</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">∈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord">0</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord">1/2</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 1em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord">4</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span></span><br>
则存在节点嵌入的放置方式满足命题3.1的条件。</p>
<p><strong>层次正交性约束</strong>:对父节点<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msup><mi>a</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>i</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a^{(i)}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.888em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.888em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>和子节点<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msup><mi>a</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>j</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>∈</mo><mtext>chi</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>i</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a^{(j)} \in \text{chi}(i)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.9271em; vertical-align: -0.0391em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.888em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.05724em;">j</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">∈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">chi</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">i</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span>:<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msup><mi>a</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>j</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>−</mo><msup><mi>a</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>i</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">⊤</mi></msup><msup><mi>a</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>i</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>=</mo><mn>0</mn><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>30</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(a^{(j)} - a^{(i)})^\top a^{(i)} = 0 \quad (30)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.188em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.938em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; <p><strong>单纯形结构约束</strong>:<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>b</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">b</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; <span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msup><mi>a</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>j</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>−</mo><msub><mi>g</mi><mi>l</mi></msub><msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">⊤</mi></msup><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msup><mi>a</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>k</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>−</mo><msub><mi>g</mi><mi>l</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo fence="true">{</mo><mtable rowspacing="0.3600em" columnalign="left left" columnspacing="1em"><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><msubsup><mi>λ</mi><mi>l</mi><mn>2</mn></msubsup><mo separator="true">,</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mi>j</mi><mo>=</mo><mi>k</mi></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mo>−</mo><mfrac><msubsup><mi>λ</mi><mi>l</mi><mn>2</mn></msubsup><mrow><mi>b</mi><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></mfrac><mo separator="true">,</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mi>j</mi><mo mathvariant="normal">≠</mo><mi>k</mi></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable></mrow><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>32</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(a^{(j)} - g_l)^\top (a^{(k)} - g_l) = \begin{cases} \lambda_l^2, &amp; j=k \\ -\frac{\lambda_l^2}{b-1}, &amp; j \neq k \end{cases} \quad (32)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.188em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="inner"><span class="mord"><span class="mrel"></span></span></span><span class="fix"></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mrel">=</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03148em;">k</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.25306em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose nulldelimiter"></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 1em;"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord">32</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span></span><br>
其中<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>g</mi><mi>l</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">g_l</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.625em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.03588em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.01968em;">l</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>是满足所有正交约束的可行原点,<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>λ</mi><mi>l</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\lambda_l</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.84444em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">λ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.01968em;">l</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>是缩放因子。</p>
<p><strong>命题3.3(深度-维度必要性)</strong></p>
<p>若深度<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>L</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">L</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">L</span></span></span></span></span>的层次结构每层有<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>b</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">b</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">b</span></span></span></span></span>个分支,则嵌入空间维度需满足:<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mi>d</mi><mo>≥</mo><mi>L</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>b</mi><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>37</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">d \geq L + b \quad (37)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83041em; vertical-align: -0.13597em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">d</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≥</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.76666em; vertical-align: -0.08333em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">L</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">b</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 1em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord">37</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p><strong>证明思路</strong>:每层的层次正交性约束<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>l</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(l+1)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.01968em;">l</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span>个仿射约束,将子节点限制在<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>d</mi><mo>−</mo><mi>l</mi><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(d-l-1)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">d</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.77777em; vertical-align: -0.08333em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.01968em;">l</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span>维子空间;嵌入<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>b</mi><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(b-1)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">b</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span>-单纯形需<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>b</mi><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(b-1)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">b</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span>维,因此要求<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>d</mi><mo>−</mo><mi>l</mi><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>≥</mo><mi>b</mi><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">d-l-1 \geq b-1</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.77777em; vertical-align: -0.08333em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">d</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.77777em; vertical-align: -0.08333em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.01968em;">l</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.78041em; vertical-align: -0.13597em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≥</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.77777em; vertical-align: -0.08333em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">b</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span></span></span></span></span>对所有深度成立。</p>
<h3 id="层次化字典与稀疏追踪">3.2 层次化字典与稀疏追踪</h3>
<p><strong>字典构造</strong>(公式5):<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mi>D</mi><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">[</mo><msup><mi>a</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo separator="true">,</mo><mo>…</mo><mo separator="true">,</mo><msup><mi>a</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>b</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo separator="true">,</mo><munder><munder><mrow><msup><mi>a</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>j</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>−</mo><msup><mi>a</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mtext>par</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>j</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo separator="true">,</mo><mo>…</mo><mo separator="true">,</mo><msup><mi>a</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>j</mi><mi>k</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>−</mo><msup><mi>a</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mtext>par</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>j</mi><mi>k</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup></mrow><mo stretchy="true">undefined</mo></munder><mtext>非根节点差向量</mtext></munder><mo stretchy="false">]</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">D = [a^{(1)}, \ldots, a^{(b)}, \underbrace{a^{(j_1)} - a^{(\text{par}(j_1))}, \ldots, a^{(j_k)} - a^{(\text{par}(j_k))}}_{\text{非根节点差向量}}]</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">D</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 2.45877em; vertical-align: -1.52077em;"></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.938em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-left: -0.05724em; margin-right: 0.0714286em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.5em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.03148em;">k</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151229em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.938em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">par</span></span><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.05724em;">j</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3448em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.34877em; margin-left: -0.05724em; margin-right: 0.0714286em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.5em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.03148em;">k</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151229em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose mtight">))</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.84244em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.52077em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p><strong>稀疏分解</strong>(公式6):任意同义词集<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>i</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">i</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.65952em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">i</span></span></span></span></span>的嵌入可表示为:<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msup><mi>a</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>i</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>=</mo><msup><mi>a</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>π</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>i</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>+</mo><munder><mo>∑</mo><mrow><mi>j</mi><mo>∈</mo><mtext>anc</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>i</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>j</mi><mo mathvariant="normal">≠</mo><msub><mi>π</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>i</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></munder><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msup><mi>a</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>j</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>−</mo><msup><mi>a</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mtext>par</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>j</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a^{(i)} = a^{(\pi_1(i))} + \sum_{j \in \text{anc}(i), j \neq \pi_1(i)} (a^{(j)} - a^{(\text{par}(j))})</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.938em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.938em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.02133em; vertical-align: -0.08333em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.938em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">π</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.317314em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.357em; margin-left: -0.03588em; margin-right: 0.0714286em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.5em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.143em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span><span class="mclose mtight">))</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 2.56601em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="inner"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mrel mtight"></span></span></span><span class="fix"></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mrel mtight">=</span></span><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">π</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.317314em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.357em; margin-left: -0.03588em; margin-right: 0.0714286em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.5em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.143em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.05em;"></span><span class=""><span class="mop op-symbol large-op">∑</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.51601em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.938em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.05724em;">j</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.188em; 其中<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>π</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>i</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\pi_1(i)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">π</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.03588em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">i</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span>是<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>i</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">i</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.65952em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">i</span></span></span></span></span>的第一祖先(根的子节点)。</p>
<p><strong>层次化OMP核心步骤</strong>:</p>
<ol>
<li>在第<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>t</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">t=0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.61508em;
