vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span></span></span></span></span>步,活跃字典<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>D</mi><mtext>active</mtext></msub><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><msub><mi>a</mi><mrow><mn>1</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>i</mi></mrow></msub><mo>:</mo><mi>i</mi><mo>∈</mo><mtext>chi</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>R</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">D_{\text{active}} = \{a_{1,i} : i \in \text{chi}(R)\}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">D</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.317502em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.02778em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">active</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.03611em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.311664em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; vertical-align: -0.0391em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">i</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">∈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; <li>在<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>t</mi><mo>&gt;</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">t&gt;0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.65418em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span></span></span></span></span>步,<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>D</mi><mtext>active</mtext></msub><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><msub><mi>a</mi><mrow><mi>l</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>j</mi></mrow></msub><mo>−</mo><msub><mi>a</mi><mrow><mi>l</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>i</mi><mtext>last</mtext></msub></mrow></msub><mo>:</mo><mi>j</mi><mo>∈</mo><mtext>chi</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>i</mi><mtext>last</mtext></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">D_{\text{active}} = \{a_{l+1,j} - a_{l,i_{\text{last}}} : j \in \text{chi}(i_{\text{last}})\}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.01968em;">l</span><span class="mpunct mtight">,</span><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3448em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.34877em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">last</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)}</span></span></span></span></span>(当前最深节点的子节点差向量)</li>
<li>计算相关性(归一化余弦相似度):<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>c</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">∣</mi><mo stretchy="false">⟨</mo><mi>r</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><msup><mi>d</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>i</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo stretchy="false">⟩</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">∣</mi></mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">∥</mi><mi>r</mi><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">∥</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mi mathvariant="normal">∥</mi><msup><mi>d</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>i</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">∥</mi><mn>2</mn></msub></mrow></mfrac></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">c_i = \frac{|\langle r, d^{(i)} \rangle|}{\|r\|_2 \|d^{(i)}\|_2}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.58056em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">c</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.311664em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 2.519em; vertical-align: -0.954em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mopen nulldelimiter"></span><span class="mfrac"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.565em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.296em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">∥</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">r</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">∥</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">2</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord">∥</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">d</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.814em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.989em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">∥</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">2</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.23em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="frac-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.677em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">∣</span><span class="mopen">⟨</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">r</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">d</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.888em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">⟩</span><span class="mord">∣</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.954em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose nulldelimiter"></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li>选择top-<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>B</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">B</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span></span></span></span></span>个候选扩展支持集,更新稀疏编码:<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msup><mi>z</mi><mo mathvariant="normal" lspace="0em" rspace="0em">′</mo></msup><mo>=</mo><mi>arg</mi><mo>⁡</mo><munder><mrow><mi>min</mi><mo>⁡</mo></mrow><mi>w</mi></munder><mi mathvariant="normal">∥</mi><mi>x</mi><mo>−</mo><msub><mi>D</mi><msup><mi>S</mi><mo mathvariant="normal" lspace="0em" rspace="0em">′</mo></msup></msub><mi>w</mi><msubsup><mi mathvariant="normal">∥</mi><mn>2</mn><mn>2</mn></msubsup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">z' = \arg\min_w \|x - D_{S'}w\|_2^2</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.801892em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.04398em;">z</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.801892em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">′</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.45em; vertical-align: -0.7em;"></span><span class="mop">ar<span style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">g</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mop op-limits"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.66786em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.4em; margin-left: 0em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.02691em;">w</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class=""><span class="mop">min</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.7em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord">∥</span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.11411em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">D</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.328331em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.02778em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.05764em;">S</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.682829em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.786em; margin-right: 0.0714286em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.5em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">′</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02691em;">w</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">∥</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.864108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.453em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">2</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">2</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.247em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li>剪枝:保留残差<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">∥</mi><msup><mi>r</mi><mo mathvariant="normal" lspace="0em" rspace="0em">′</mo></msup><msubsup><mi mathvariant="normal">∥</mi><mn>2</mn><mn>2</mn></msubsup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\|r'\|_2^2</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.06411em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">∥</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">r</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.751892em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">′</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">∥</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.814108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.45189em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">2</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">2</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.248108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>最小的<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>B</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">B</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span></span></span></span></span>个假设</li>
</ol>
<p><strong>命题4.1(ERC成功区域扩大,非正式版本)</strong></p>
<p>假设Hierarchical OMP每次迭代选择的原子都在正确支持集中,则其精确恢复系数(ERC)成功区域严格大于全字典上的OMP:<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mtext>ERC</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mover accent="true"><mi>D</mi><mo>^</mo></mover><mo separator="true">;</mo><mi>S</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">∣</mi><msub><mi>T</mi><mi>L</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>&lt;</mo><mtext>ERC</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mover accent="true"><mi>D</mi><mo>^</mo></mover><mo separator="true">;</mo><mi>S</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\text{ERC}(\hat{D}; S | T_L) &lt; \text{ERC}(\hat{D}; S)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.19677em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">ERC</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord accent"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.94677em;"><span class="" style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">D</span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.25233em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="accent-body" style="left: -0.19444em;"><span class="mord">^</span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">;</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05764em;">S</span><span class="mord">∣</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">T</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.328331em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.13889em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">L</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">&lt;</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.19677em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">ERC</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord accent"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.94677em;"><span class="" style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">D</span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.25233em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="accent-body" style="left: -0.19444em;"><span class="mord">^</span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">;</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05764em;">S</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span></span><br>
其中<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>T</mi><mi>L</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">T_L</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">T</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.328331em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.13889em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">L</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>是子树限制集合,<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mover accent="true"><mi>D</mi><mo>^</mo></mover></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\hat{D}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.94677em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord accent"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.94677em;"><span class="" style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">D</span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.25233em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="accent-body" style="left: -0.19444em;"><span class="mord">^</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>是列归一化字典。</p>
<hr>
<h2 id="四、实验设计与关键数据">四、实验设计与关键数据</h2>
<h3 id="合成实验">合成实验</h3>
<ul>
<li><strong>设置</strong>:<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>b</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>3</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">b=3</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">b</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">3</span></span></span></span></span>, <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>L</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>7</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">L=7</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">L</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">7</span></span></span></span></span>, <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>d</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>50</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">d=50</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">d</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">50</span></span></span></span></span>, 2187个叶节点, 每叶5个样本</li>
<li><strong>结果</strong>(图5):稀疏度<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>k</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>8</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">k=8</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03148em;">k</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">8</span></span></span></span></span>时,Hierarchical OMP精度/召回率约<strong>0.95/0.95</strong>,OMP仅<strong>0.2/0.6</strong></li>
</ul>
<h3 id="imagenet实验">ImageNet实验</h3>
<ul>
<li><strong>关键数据</strong>(表1,稀疏度14):
<ul>
<li>12-shot: HCEP准确率<strong>52.1%</strong>/精度<strong>71.2%</strong>/召回<strong>71.8%</strong> vs OMP <strong>45.8%/15.6%/36.6%</strong></li>
<li>Full数据: HCEP <strong>65.2%/70.1%/71.1%</strong> vs CBM <strong>78.5%/45.6%/97.3%</strong>(CBM准确率高但概念精度低)</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="cifar-100imagenette">CIFAR-100/ImageNette</h3>
<ul>
<li>ImageNette(图8下):稀疏度5时,HCEP精度/召回**<sub>0.95/0.9**,OMP仅**</sub>0.65/0.4**</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="运行时分析">运行时分析</h3>
<ul>
<li><strong>图9</strong>:束宽<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>B</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">B</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span></span></span></span></span>从1增至32,支持集精度从<sub>25%升至</sub>55%,运行时仅从<sub>5ms增至</sub>18ms(GPU并行化)</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<h2 id="五、未来研究方向与机会">五、未来研究方向与机会</h2>
<h3 id="学术探索">学术探索</h3>
<ul>
<li><strong>非欧几何嵌入</strong>:深层次结构在欧氏空间中锥角趋小,双曲空间可能更适合</li>
<li><strong>噪声层次结构</strong>:通过<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi><mn>1</mn></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\ell_1</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.84444em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">ℓ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>正则化插值层次化/非层次化解决方案</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="技术机会">技术机会</h3>
<ul>
<li><strong>层次感知微调</strong>:在预训练模型中注入层次几何约束</li>
<li><strong>自动层次构建</strong>:利用LLM改进分类法归纳质量(如CIFAR-100实验)</li>
<li><strong>跨域应用</strong>:将框架扩展至医疗(RadLex)、生物(iNaturalist)等领域</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="投资方向">投资方向</h3>
<ul>
<li>低样本学习场景下的可解释AI工具</li>
<li>高风险决策系统的可信AI基础设施</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<h2 id="六、批判性分析">六、批判性分析</h2>
<h3 id="不足之处">不足之处</h3>
<ul>
<li><strong>维度限制</strong>:命题3.3要求<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>d</mi><mo>≥</mo><mi>L</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>b</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">d \geq L+b</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83041em; vertical-align: -0.13597em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">d</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≥</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.76666em; vertical-align: -0.08333em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">L</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">b</span></span></span></span></span>,对极深或高分支因子层次结构限制性强</li>
<li><strong>层次质量依赖</strong>:CIFAR-100需用LLM构建层次(质量不如WordNet),可能产生错误解释路径</li>
<li><strong>计算复杂度</strong>:Hierarchical OMP为<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>O</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>T</mi><mi>B</mi><mi>K</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">∣</mi><msub><mi>D</mi><mtext>active</mtext></msub><mi mathvariant="normal">∣</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">O(TBK|D_{\text{active}}|)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">O</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">TB</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">K</span><span class="mord">∣</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">D</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.317502em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.02778em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">active</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord">∣</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span>,大分支因子下计算昂贵(虽可GPU并行)</li>
<li><strong>异常值处理</strong>:假设输入属于已知类,对全新类别无法处理(需先扩展层次)</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="需验证之处">需验证之处</h3>
<ul>
<li>单纯形结构在实际CLIP嵌入中的精确程度(论文仅验证正交性)</li>
<li>命题4.1的"原子选择正确"假设在噪声数据下是否成立</li>
<li>跨不同视觉-语言模型的泛化性(仅测试CLIP/SigLIP)</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<h2 id="七、可借鉴的创新与启发">七、可借鉴的创新与启发</h2>
<h3 id="重点学习内容">重点学习内容</h3>
<ol>
<li><strong>几何约束设计</strong>:将语义层次转化为可验证的几何条件(锥体、正交性、单纯形)</li>
<li><strong>差向量语义化</strong>:将"概念"定义为差向量而非绝对嵌入,避免平凡解</li>
<li><strong>束搜索缓解错误传播</strong>:维护多假设而非贪心单路径</li>
</ol>
<h3 id="启发">启发</h3>
<ul>
<li>在其他结构化数据(如知识图谱)中应用类似几何约束</li>
<li>将层次先验编码进损失函数,而非后处理阶段</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="补充知识">补充知识</h3>
<ul>
<li><strong>稀疏编码理论</strong>:互相干性(mutual coherence)、RIP条件</li>
<li><strong>双曲几何</strong>:Poincaré嵌入在层次表示中的应用</li>
<li><strong>WordNet</strong>:理解其DAG结构(非严格树)对多路径处理的影响</li>
</ul>
<h1 id="双曲几何与欧几里得k-means在广义类别发现中的对比研究——深度解读">双曲几何与欧几里得K-means在广义类别发现中的对比研究——深度解读</h1>
<h2 id="一、论文核心创新与贡献1200字">一、论文核心创新与贡献(1200字)</h2>
<p>这篇论文聚焦于<strong>广义类别发现(Generalized Category Discovery, GCD)<strong>任务,针对现有双曲表示学习方法的一个关键缺陷:虽然在</strong>表示学习阶段</strong>使用双曲几何,但在<strong>聚类阶段</strong>却回退到欧几里得空间,导致学到的层次结构信息被扭曲。</p>
<h3 id="研究动机">研究动机</h3>
<p>GCD任务要求模型同时对<strong>已见类(seen classes)<strong>和</strong>未见类(unseen classes)<strong>进行聚类。作者指出,数据中普遍存在</strong>隐式层次结构</strong>(如"动物→哺乳动物→猫"),而双曲几何由于其<strong>指数增长特性</strong>天然适合表示这种树状层次(Gromov, 1987)。然而,先前方法如<strong>HypCD</strong>(Liu et al., 2025a)和<strong>HIDISC</strong>(Rathore et al., 2025)都存在一个悖论:</p>
<blockquote>
<p>“所有双曲学习的非参数方法都诉诸于在<strong>欧几里得嵌入</strong>上进行聚类,而非双曲空间(Liu et al., 2025a; Rathore et al., 2025)。这可能导致学到的层次结构失真,因为欧几里得几何并非表示这些层次的最优选择(Gromov, 1987)。”</p>
</blockquote>
<h3 id="核心方法hc-gcd框架">核心方法:HC-GCD框架</h3>
<p>论文提出<strong>Hyperbolic Clustered GCD (HC-GCD)</strong>,包含三个关键组件:</p>
<p><strong>1. Lorentz超双曲面模型中的表示学习</strong></p>
<p>选择Lorentz模型而非Poincaré球模型的原因是:<strong>存在闭式质心</strong>(closed-form centroid)。Lorentz超双曲面定义为:</p>
<p><span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msubsup><mi mathvariant="script">H</mi><mi>κ</mi><mi>n</mi></msubsup><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo fence="true">{</mo><mi>x</mi><mo>∈</mo><msup><mi mathvariant="double-struck">R</mi><mrow><mi>n</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup><mo>∣</mo><mo stretchy="false">⟨</mo><mi>x</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>x</mi><msub><mo stretchy="false">⟩</mo><mi>L</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mo>−</mo><mfrac><mn>1</mn><mi>κ</mi></mfrac><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>x</mi><mn>0</mn></msub><mo>&gt;</mo><mn>0</mn><mo fence="true">}</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{H}^n_\kappa = \left\{ x \in \mathbb{R}^{n+1} \mid \langle x, x \rangle_L = -\frac{1}{\kappa}, x_0 &gt; 0 \right\}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.961392em; vertical-align: -0.247em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right: 0.00965em;">H</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.714392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.453em; margin-left: -0.00965em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">κ</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">n</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.247em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 2.40003em; vertical-align: -0.95003em;"></span><span class="minner"><span class="mopen delimcenter" style="top: 0em;"><span class="delimsizing size3">{</span></span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">∈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbb">R</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.864108em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">n</span><span class="mbin mtight">+</span><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">∣</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mopen">⟨</span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mclose"><span class="mclose">⟩</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.328331em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">L</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord">−</span><span class="mord"><span class="mopen nulldelimiter"></span><span class="mfrac"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.32144em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.314em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">κ</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.23em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="frac-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.677em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.686em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose nulldelimiter"></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">0</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">&gt;</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span><span class="mclose delimcenter" style="top: 0em;"><span class="delimsizing size3">}</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>其中Lorentz内积为:<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">⟨</mo><mi>x</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>y</mi><msub><mo stretchy="false">⟩</mo><mi>L</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mo>−</mo><msub><mi>x</mi><mn>0</mn></msub><msub><mi>y</mi><mn>0</mn></msub><mo>+</mo><mo stretchy="false">⟨</mo><msub><mi>x</mi><mrow><mi>s</mi><mi>p</mi><mi>a</mi><mi>c</mi><mi>e</mi></mrow></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>y</mi><mrow><mi>s</mi><mi>p</mi><mi>a</mi><mi>c</mi><mi>e</mi></mrow></msub><mo stretchy="false">⟩</mo><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>2</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\langle x, y \rangle_L = -x_0 y_0 + \langle x_{space}, y_{space} \rangle \quad (2)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">⟨</span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span><span class="mclose"><span class="mclose">⟩</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.328331em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">L</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.77777em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord">−</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">0</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.03588em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">0</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.03611em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mopen">⟨</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">s</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">p</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">a</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">ce</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.03588em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">s</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">p</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">a</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">ce</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">⟩</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 1em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord">2</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p><strong>2. 双曲K-means算法</strong></p>
<p>算法的核心挑战是定义<strong>距离函数</strong>和<strong>质心</strong>。论文使用:</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>距离函数</strong>(公式4):Lorentz超双曲面距离<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>d</mi><mi>H</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>y</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><msqrt><mfrac><mn>1</mn><mi>κ</mi></mfrac></msqrt><msup><mrow><mi>cosh</mi><mo>⁡</mo></mrow><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mo>−</mo><mi>κ</mi><mo stretchy="false">⟨</mo><mi>x</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>y</mi><msub><mo stretchy="false">⟩</mo><mi>L</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">d_H(x,y) = \sqrt{\frac{1}{\kappa}} \cosh^{-1}(-\kappa \langle x, y \rangle_L)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">d</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.328331em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.08125em;">H</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 2.44em; <p><strong>质心</strong>:Lorentz质心(公式11)<br>

<p><strong>3. 数学严格性证明</strong></p>
<p>论文最重要的理论贡献是<strong>定理1</strong>:证明了<strong>Einstein中点</strong>(Klein模型中的质心)等价于<strong>Lorentz质心</strong>的投影。这保证了在Lorentz超双曲面上直接计算质心的合理性,无需在不同双曲模型间转换。证明思路如下:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>引理1</strong>:建立Klein模型到Lorentz超双曲面的映射(公式14)</li>
<li><strong>推论1.1</strong>:证明Einstein中点中的Lorentz因子<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>γ</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><msqrt><mi>κ</mi></msqrt><msub><mi>x</mi><mrow><mi>t</mi><mi>i</mi><mi>m</mi><mi>e</mi></mrow></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\gamma_i = \sqrt{\kappa} x_{time}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.625em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05556em;">γ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.311664em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; </ul>
<h3 id="实验设计与关键发现">实验设计与关键发现</h3>
<p>在**语义偏移基准(Semantic Shift Benchmark)**的三个细粒度数据集(CUB鸟类、Stanford Cars、FGVC-Aircraft)上进行实验:</p>
<p><strong>表1核心数据</strong>:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>CUB数据集</strong>: HC-GCD(双曲K-means) <strong>71.70%</strong> vs Hyp-GCD <strong>71.52%</strong> (All准确率)</li>
<li><strong>Stanford Cars</strong>: HC-GCD <strong>73.69%</strong> vs Hyp-GCD <strong>68.31%</strong> (提升<strong>5.38个百分点</strong>)</li>
<li><strong>FGVC-Aircraft</strong>: HC-GCD <strong>61.90%</strong> vs Hyp-GCD <strong>59.36%</strong></li>
</ul>
<p>更重要的是<strong>稳定性改进</strong>:HC-GCD的标准差显著更低(如CUB数据集上<strong>0.55%</strong> vs <strong>2.06%</strong>),表明训练更稳定。</p>
<p><strong>消融实验亮点</strong>:</p>
<ol>
<li>
<p><strong>欧几里得裁剪影响</strong>(表2):移除嵌入裁剪在FGVC-Aircraft上准确率从<strong>61.90%<strong>升至</strong>64.72%</strong>,但在其他数据集下降,表明该操作具有<strong>数据集依赖性</strong></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>标签粒度一致性</strong>(表4):使用FGVC-Aircraft的三层粒度(制造商→系列→变体)测试同质性指标,HC-GCD在所有粒度上都达到最高(<strong>90.46%/89.09%/82.48%</strong>),超过Hyp-GCD <strong>3-4个百分点</strong>,证明<strong>双曲聚类更好地保持了层次结构</strong></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Poincaré模型失败</strong>:尝试在Poincaré球模型上使用双曲K-means导致<strong>准确率接近零</strong>,所有样本被分配到单一质心,说明需要进一步研究不同双曲模型的聚类可行性</p>
</li>
</ol>
<hr>
<h2 id="二、研究目标与实际意义-1">二、研究目标与实际意义</h2>
<h3 id="研究目标-1">研究目标</h3>
<ul>
<li><strong>核心问题</strong>:现有双曲GCD方法在聚类阶段放弃双曲几何,回退到欧几里得空间,损失层次信息</li>
<li><strong>解决方案</strong>:在Lorentz超双曲面上直接进行K-means聚类,保持端到端的双曲几何表示</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="产业意义-1">产业意义</h3>
<ul>
<li><strong>开放世界分类</strong>:在医疗诊断、物种识别等场景中,需要同时处理已知和新类别</li>
<li><strong>层次感知推荐</strong>:电商、内容推荐中利用商品/内容的层次结构提升泛化能力</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<h2 id="三、模型方法详解-1">三、模型方法详解</h2>
<h3 id="lorentz超双曲面几何">3.1 Lorentz超双曲面几何</h3>
<p><strong>定义</strong>(公式1):上超双曲面的上半支<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msubsup><mi mathvariant="script">H</mi><mi>κ</mi><mi>n</mi></msubsup><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi>x</mi><mo>∈</mo><msup><mi mathvariant="double-struck">R</mi><mrow><mi>n</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup><mo>∣</mo><mo stretchy="false">⟨</mo><mi>x</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>x</mi><msub><mo stretchy="false">⟩</mo><mi>L</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mo>−</mo><mfrac><mn>1</mn><mi>κ</mi></mfrac><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>x</mi><mn>0</mn></msub><mo>&gt;</mo><mn>0</mn><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{H}^n_\kappa = \{ x \in \mathbb{R}^{n+1} \mid \langle x, x \rangle_L = -\frac{1}{\kappa}, x_0 &gt; 0 \}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.961392em; vertical-align: -0.247em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right: 0.00965em;">H</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.714392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.453em; <p><strong>Lorentz内积</strong>(公式2):引入时间维度<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">⟨</mo><msub><mi>x</mi><mi>H</mi></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>y</mi><mi>H</mi></msub><msub><mo stretchy="false">⟩</mo><mi>L</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mo>−</mo><msub><mi>x</mi><mrow><mi>t</mi><mi>i</mi><mi>m</mi><mi>e</mi></mrow></msub><msub><mi>y</mi><mrow><mi>t</mi><mi>i</mi><mi>m</mi><mi>e</mi></mrow></msub><mo>+</mo><mo stretchy="false">⟨</mo><msub><mi>x</mi><mrow><mi>s</mi><mi>p</mi><mi>a</mi><mi>c</mi><mi>e</mi></mrow></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>y</mi><mrow><mi>s</mi><mi>p</mi><mi>a</mi><mi>c</mi><mi>e</mi></mrow></msub><mo stretchy="false">⟩</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\langle x_H, y_H \rangle_L = -x_{time} y_{time} + \langle x_{space}, y_{space} \rangle</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; <p><strong>时间分量约束</strong>(公式3):由双曲面约束导出<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>x</mi><mrow><mi>t</mi><mi>i</mi><mi>m</mi><mi>e</mi></mrow></msub><mo>=</mo><msqrt><mrow><mn>1</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><mi>κ</mi><mo>+</mo><mo stretchy="false">⟨</mo><msub><mi>x</mi><mrow><mi>s</mi><mi>p</mi><mi>a</mi><mi>c</mi><mi>e</mi></mrow></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>x</mi><mrow><mi>s</mi><mi>p</mi><mi>a</mi><mi>c</mi><mi>e</mi></mrow></msub><mo stretchy="false">⟩</mo></mrow></msqrt></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">x_{time} = \sqrt{1/\kappa + \langle x_{space}, x_{space} \rangle}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.58056em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">s</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">p</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">a</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">ce</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">⟩</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.22582em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.8em;"></span><span class="hide-tail" style="min-width: 1.02em; <p><strong>距离函数</strong>(公式4):<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>d</mi><mi>H</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>y</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><msqrt><mfrac><mn>1</mn><mi>κ</mi></mfrac></msqrt><msup><mrow><mi>cosh</mi><mo>⁡</mo></mrow><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mo>−</mo><mi>κ</mi><mo stretchy="false">⟨</mo><mi>x</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>y</mi><msub><mo stretchy="false">⟩</mo><mi>L</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">d_H(x,y) = \sqrt{\frac{1}{\kappa}} \cosh^{-1}(-\kappa \langle x, y \rangle_L)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; <h3 id="klein模型与einstein中点">3.2 Klein模型与Einstein中点</h3>

<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msubsup><mi mathvariant="script">K</mi><mi>κ</mi><mi>n</mi></msubsup><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi>x</mi><mo>∈</mo><msup><mi mathvariant="double-struck">R</mi><mi>n</mi></msup><mo separator="true">;</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">∥</mi><mi>x</mi><msup><mi mathvariant="normal">∥</mi><mn>2</mn></msup><mo>&lt;</mo><mfrac><mn>1</mn><mi>κ</mi></mfrac><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{K}^n_\kappa = \{ x \in \mathbb{R}^n ; <p><strong>投影映射</strong>(公式6):<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>x</mi><mi>K</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mfrac><msub><mi>x</mi><mrow><mi>s</mi><mi>p</mi><mi>a</mi><mi>c</mi><mi>e</mi></mrow></msub><mrow><msqrt><mi>κ</mi></msqrt><msub><mi>x</mi><mrow><mi>t</mi><mi>i</mi><mi>m</mi><mi>e</mi></mrow></msub></mrow></mfrac></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">x_K = \frac{x_{space}}{\sqrt{\kappa} x_{time}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.58056em; <p><strong>Einstein中点</strong>(公式8-9):利用Klein模型测地线为直线的性质<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>μ</mi><mi>K</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mrow><munder><mo>∑</mo><mrow><mi>i</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></munder><msub><mi>γ</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><msub><mi>x</mi><mrow><mi>K</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>i</mi></mrow></msub></mrow><mrow><munder><mo>∑</mo><mrow><mi>i</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></munder><msub><mi>γ</mi><mi>i</mi></msub></mrow></mfrac><mo separator="true">,</mo><mspace width="1em"></mspace><msub><mi>γ</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mn>1</mn><msqrt><mrow><mn>1</mn><mo>−</mo><mi>κ</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">∥</mi><msub><mi>x</mi><mrow><mi>K</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>i</mi></mrow></msub><msup><mi mathvariant="normal">∥</mi><mn>2</mn></msup></mrow></msqrt></mfrac></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mu_K = \frac{\sum_{i=1} \gamma_i x_{K,i}}{\sum_{i=1} \gamma_i}, \quad \gamma_i = \frac{1}{\sqrt{1 - \kappa \|x_{K,i}\|^2}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.625em; <h3 id="双曲k-means核心定理">3.3 双曲K-means核心定理</h3>
<p><strong>Lorentz质心</strong>(公式11):<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>μ</mi><mi>H</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mn>1</mn><msqrt><mi>κ</mi></msqrt></mfrac><mfrac><mrow><munder><mo>∑</mo><mrow><mi>i</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></munder><msub><mi>w</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><msub><mi>x</mi><mrow><mi>H</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>i</mi></mrow></msub></mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">∣</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">∥</mi><munder><mo>∑</mo><mrow><mi>i</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></munder><msub><mi>w</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><msub><mi>x</mi><mrow><mi>H</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>i</mi></mrow></msub><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">∥</mi><mi>L</mi></msub><mi mathvariant="normal">∣</mi></mrow></mfrac></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mu_H = \frac{1}{\sqrt{\kappa}} \frac{\sum_{i=1} w_i x_{H,i}}{|\|\sum_{i=1} w_i x_{H,i}\|_L|}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.625em; <p>该质心最小化<strong>Lorentzian距离平方</strong>:<br>

<h3 id="hc-gcd训练流程">3.4 HC-GCD训练流程</h3>
<p><strong>对比损失</strong>(公式23-24):结合自监督和监督损失<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msubsup><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mrow><mi>σ</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>i</mi></mrow><mi>u</mi></msubsup><mo>=</mo><mo>−</mo><mi>log</mi><mo>⁡</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>σ</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>i</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><msubsup><mi>z</mi><mrow><mi>H</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>i</mi></mrow><mo mathvariant="normal" lspace="0em" rspace="0em">′</mo></msubsup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}^u_{\sigma,i} = -\log(\sigma(i, z'_{H,i}))</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.0975em; <p><strong>距离对比分数</strong>(公式25):<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>σ</mi><mi>D</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>i</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>y</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mrow><mi>exp</mi><mo>⁡</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mo>−</mo><msub><mi>d</mi><mi>H</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>z</mi><mrow><mi>H</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>i</mi></mrow></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>y</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><mi>τ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mrow><munder><mo>∑</mo><mi>n</mi></munder><msub><mn mathvariant="double-struck">1</mn><mrow><mo stretchy="false">[</mo><mi>n</mi><mo mathvariant="normal">≠</mo><mi>i</mi><mo stretchy="false">]</mo></mrow></msub><mi>exp</mi><mo>⁡</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mo>−</mo><msub><mi>d</mi><mi>H</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>z</mi><mrow><mi>H</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>i</mi></mrow></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>z</mi><mrow><mi>H</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>n</mi></mrow></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><mi>τ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mfrac></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\sigma_D(i,y) = \frac{\exp(-d_H(z_{H,i}, y)/\tau)}{\sum_n \mathbb{1}_{[n \neq i]} \exp(-d_H(z_{H,i}, z_{H,n})/\tau)}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; <p><strong>角度对比分数</strong>(公式26-27):使用MERU的外角<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mtext>ext</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>y</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><msup><mrow><mi>cos</mi><mo>⁡</mo></mrow><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup><mrow><mo fence="true">(</mo><mfrac><mrow><msub><mi>y</mi><mrow><mi>t</mi><mi>i</mi><mi>m</mi><mi>e</mi></mrow></msub><mo>+</mo><msub><mi>x</mi><mrow><mi>t</mi><mi>i</mi><mi>m</mi><mi>e</mi></mrow></msub><mi>κ</mi><mo stretchy="false">⟨</mo><mi>x</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>y</mi><msub><mo stretchy="false">⟩</mo><mi>L</mi></msub></mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">∥</mi><msub><mi>x</mi><mrow><mi>s</mi><mi>p</mi><mi>a</mi><mi>c</mi><mi>e</mi></mrow></msub><mi mathvariant="normal">∥</mi><msqrt><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>κ</mi><mo stretchy="false">⟨</mo><mi>x</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>y</mi><msub><mo stretchy="false">⟩</mo><mi>L</mi></msub><msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mn>2</mn></msup><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msqrt></mrow></mfrac><mo fence="true">)</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\text{ext}(x,y) = \cos^{-1}\left( \frac{y_{time} + x_{time}\kappa\langle x,y \rangle_L}{\|x_{space}\| \sqrt{(\kappa\langle x,y \rangle_L)^2 - 1}} \right)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; <p><strong>总损失</strong>(公式28-30):线性衰减<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>α</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\alpha</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0037em;">α</span></span></span></span></span>从1到0<br>

<h2 id="四、实验设计与关键结果">四、实验设计与关键结果</h2>
<h3 id="数据集">数据集</h3>
<p><strong>语义偏移基准</strong>(Vaze et al., 2022b):</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>CUB</strong>: 200种鸟类,100个已见类</li>
<li><strong>Stanford Cars</strong>: 196种车型,98个已见类</li>
<li><strong>FGVC-Aircraft</strong>: 100种飞机,50个已见类</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="模型配置">模型配置</h3>
<ul>
<li><strong>骨干网络</strong>: ViT-B14 + DINOv2预训练</li>

<li><strong>裁剪范数</strong>: 2.3</li>
<li><strong>曲率</strong>: <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>c</mi><mo>=</mo><mo>−</mo><mn>0.05</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">c = -0.05</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">c</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.72777em; vertical-align: -0.08333em;"></span><span class="mord">−</span><span class="mord">0.05</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li><strong>训练</strong>: SGD优化器,余弦退火学习率(0.1→0.0001),200轮</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="五、未来研究方向与技术机会">五、未来研究方向与技术机会</h2>
<h3 id="学术探索-1">学术探索</h3>
<ul>
<li><strong>多模型双曲聚类</strong>:解决Poincaré模型聚类失败问题(当前准确率接近0)</li>
<li><strong>自适应曲率学习</strong>:当前固定<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>c</mi><mo>=</mo><mo>−</mo><mn>0.05</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">c=-0.05</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">c</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.72777em; vertical-align: -0.08333em;"></span><span class="mord">−</span><span class="mord">0.05</span></span></span></span></span>,可探索数据驱动的曲率选择</li>
<li><strong>混合几何模型</strong>:结合双曲(层次)、欧几里得(平面)、球面(周期)特性</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="技术机会-1">技术机会</h3>
<ul>
<li><strong>层次感知推荐系统</strong>:利用商品/内容的双曲嵌入实现更精准的多粒度推荐</li>
<li><strong>零样本学习</strong>:双曲几何天然适合处理未见类别的层次泛化</li>
<li><strong>知识图谱嵌入</strong>:将GCD框架扩展至实体/关系的联合聚类</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="投资方向-1">投资方向</h3>
<ul>
<li>低资源场景下的开放世界分类工具(如生物多样性监测)</li>
<li>医疗影像的层次化诊断系统(疾病分类学)</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<h2 id="六、批判性分析-1">六、批判性分析</h2>
<h3 id="主要不足">主要不足</h3>
<ol>
<li>
<p><strong>方法覆盖有限</strong>:论文明确指出未适配领先的非参数方法(如Hyp-SelEx),仅关注基础GCD模型以隔离双曲聚类效果</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Poincaré失败未解释</strong>:在Poincaré球模型上双曲K-means完全失败(所有样本分配到单一质心),论文未深入分析根本原因,仅表示"需要进一步研究"</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>裁剪操作矛盾</strong>:表2显示移除欧几里得裁剪在不同数据集上效果相反(FGVC提升3%,CUB下降3%),缺乏理论解释</p>
</li>
</ol>
<h3 id="需验证之处-1">需验证之处</h3>
<ul>
<li><strong>定理1的数值稳定性</strong>:公式11中的Lorentz范数<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">∥</mi><mo>⋅</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">∥</mi><mi>L</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\|\cdot\|_L</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">∥</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">⋅</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">∥</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.328331em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">L</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>在分母,可能导致数值不稳定(虽然实验未报告此问题)</li>
<li><strong>计算复杂度</strong>:未报告双曲K-means相对欧几里得的时间开销</li>
<li><strong>超参数敏感性</strong>:曲率<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>c</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">c</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">c</span></span></span></span></span>和裁剪范数<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>r</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">r</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">r</span></span></span></span></span>的选择是否对所有数据集普适</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="潜在问题">潜在问题</h3>
<ul>
<li><strong>理论-实践差距</strong>:Lorentz质心最小化<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msubsup><mi>d</mi><mi>L</mi><mn>2</mn></msubsup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">d^2_L</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.08944em; vertical-align: -0.275331em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">d</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.814108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.42467em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">L</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">2</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.275331em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>而非<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msubsup><mi>d</mi><mi>H</mi><mn>2</mn></msubsup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">d^2_H</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.08944em; vertical-align: -0.275331em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">d</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.814108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.42467em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.08125em;">H</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">d</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.328331em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.08125em;">H</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>聚类,理论保证的适用性存疑</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<h2 id="七、可借鉴的创新与启发-1">七、可借鉴的创新与启发</h2>
<h3 id="重点学习内容-1">重点学习内容</h3>
<ol>
<li>
<p><strong>几何模型选择的实用主义</strong>:选择Lorentz而非Poincaré的核心理由是"存在闭式质心",体现了理论工具选择的工程导向</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>跨模型等价性证明</strong>:定理1建立Einstein中点与Lorentz质心的等价,避免了模型间转换开销,这种"懒惰求值"思想值得借鉴</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>多粒度评估</strong>:表4的标签粒度分析(制造商→系列→变体)巧妙验证了层次结构保持能力,比单一准确率更具说服力</p>
</li>
</ol>
<h3 id="启发-1">启发</h3>
<ul>
<li><strong>双曲几何的"全栈"使用</strong>:从表示学习到聚类保持一致几何,避免空间切换损失</li>
<li><strong>稳定性作为评估指标</strong>:表1的标准差对比凸显了训练稳定性的重要性,尤其在开放世界场景</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="补充知识-1">补充知识</h3>
<ul>
<li><strong>双曲几何基础</strong>:Lorentz、Poincaré、Klein模型的几何性质与转换关系</li>
<li><strong>测地线与质心</strong>:不同几何空间中质心的定义与计算方法</li>
<li><strong>GCD任务</strong>:已见/未见类联合聚类的评估协议(clustering accuracy, homogeneity)</li>
</ul>
